<div class="js-tweet-text-container">
  <p class="TweetTextSize TweetTextSize--normal js-tweet-text tweet-text" lang="en" data-aria-label-part="4">Today has not been a great day for cohesion and tolerance in the national conversation.   <p class="TweetTextSize TweetTextSize--normal js-tweet-text tweet-text" lang="en" data-aria-label-part="0">Local elections in May will decide how local services are run - and how much you pay for them. 

Things like street cleaning <img class="Emoji Emoji--forText" src="https://abs.twimg.com/emoji/v2/72x72/267b.png" draggable="false" alt="" title="Universal recycling symbol" aria-label="Emoji: Universal recycling symbol" />rubbish collection <img class="Emoji Emoji--forText" src="https://abs.twimg.com/emoji/v2/72x72/1f5d1.png" draggable="false" alt="" title="Wastebasket" aria-label="Emoji: Wastebasket" />road repairs <img class="Emoji Emoji--forText" src="https://abs.twimg.com/emoji/v2/72x72/1f697.png" draggable="false" alt="" title="Automobile" aria-label="Emoji: Automobile" />&amp; helping the elderly <img class="Emoji Emoji--forText" src="https://abs.twimg.com/emoji/v2/72x72/1f475.png" draggable="false" alt="" title="Older woman" aria-label="Emoji: Older woman" />

Conservative councillors deliver better services in your area and lower taxes for you.<a href="https://t.co/SBDbQ6XRBZ" class="twitter-timeline-link u-hidden" data-pre-embedded="true" dir="ltr">pic.twitter.com/SBDbQ6XRBZ</a></p>

French authorities are regarding her murder as an antisemitic hate crime.<a href="https://t.co/of5UdyD2m6" class="twitter-timeline-link u-hidden" data-pre-embedded="true" dir="ltr">pic.twitter.com/of5UdyD2m6</a></p>
